<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сушить.html>суши́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sušítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сушка.html>су́шка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">súška</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сушка.html>су́шки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сушка.html>су́шки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сушка.html>су́шек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>drying (process); desiccation</li>
<li>sooshka / sushka, ring-shaped cracknel, bagel</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сушняк.html>сушня́к</a> (23053)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сушить.html>су́ша</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">súša</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-няк</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-njak</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сушняк.html>сушня́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sušnják</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сушняк.html>сушняка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сушняк.html>сушняки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сушняк.html>сушняко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">collective</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dry leaves, dry branches</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> strong thirst, such as the next day after a drinking party</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dry wine</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:существенный.html>суще́ственно</a> (7062)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:существенный.html>суще́ственный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">suščéstvennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:существенный.html>суще́ственный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">suščéstvennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:существо.html>существо́</a> (1250)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>су́щий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">súščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ество</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-estvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:существо.html>существо́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">suščestvó</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:существо.html>существа́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:существо.html>существа́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:существо.html>суще́ств</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>creature, being</li>
<li>essence</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The noun <b><a href = vnd.unilang:существо.html>существо́</a></b> is one of the rare Russian neuter nouns to have animacy. Other neuter nouns with animacy include <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:животный.html>живо́тное</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">živótnoje</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насекомое.html>насеко́мое</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nasekómoje</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, etc.</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:существовавший.html>существова́вший</a> (577)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:существовавший.html>существова́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">suščestvovávšij</span>)
</p>

***сфера.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сфера.html>сфе́ра</a> (2097)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сфера.html>сфе́ра</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sféra</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сфера.html>сфе́ры</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сфера.html>сфе́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сфера.html>сфе́р</a></b>)
</p>

***схватить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:схватить.html>схвати́ть</a> (1074)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хвати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xvatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:схватить.html>схвати́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sxvatítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хватать.html>хвата́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:схватывать.html>схва́тывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to grasp, to grab, to seize, to snap, to snatch, to catch, to catch hold of
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:схватить.html>схвати́ть</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sxvatítʹ</b> kovó-libo zá ruku/za rúku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to seize / grasp someone by the hand</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:схватить.html>схвати́ть</a></b> что́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лето.html>лету́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sxvatítʹ</b> štó-libo na letú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be very quick at something</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:схватить.html>схвати́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:попасть.html>попа́ло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sxvatítʹ</b> što popálo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to seize up whatever comes to hand</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:схватить.html>схвати́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душу</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>ду́шу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sxvatítʹ</b> zá dušu/za dúšu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to tug at one's heart-strings</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:схватить.html>схвати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sxvatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:схватиться.html>схвати́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sxvatítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">схва́тываться</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хвататься.html>хвата́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to seize, to hold</li>
<li>to grapple with, to come to blows with, to skirmish with
<dl><dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">схва́тываться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sxvátyvatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:схватить.html>схвати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sxvatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>
<li><i>(paint or glue)</i> to grab, to grip, <i>(cement)</i> to set, to stiffen
<dl><dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">схва́тываться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sxvátyvatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:схватка.html>схва́тка</a> (5061)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:схватить.html>схвати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sxvatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:схватка.html>схва́тка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sxvátka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:схватка.html>схва́тки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:схватка.html>схва́тки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:схватка.html>схва́ток</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>skirmish, fight, combat, encounter</li>
<li>scuffle, squabble</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> contraction <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a strong and often painful shortening of the uterine muscles prior to or during childbirth</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***схватывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:схватывать.html>схва́тывать</a> (16622)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:схватить.html>схвати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sxvatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:схватывать.html>схва́тывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sxvátyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:схватить.html>схвати́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to grasp, to grab, to seize, to snap, to snatch, to catch, to catch hold of
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:схватывать.html>схва́тывать</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sxvátyvatʹ</b> kovó-libo zá ruku/za rúku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to seize / grasp someone by the hand</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:схватывать.html>схва́тывать</a></b> что́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лето.html>лету́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sxvátyvatʹ</b> štó-libo na letú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be very quick at something</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:схватывать.html>схва́тывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:попасть.html>попа́ло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sxvátyvatʹ</b> što popálo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to seize up whatever comes to hand</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:схватывать.html>схва́тывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душу</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>ду́шу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sxvátyvatʹ</b> zá dušu/za dúšu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to tug at one's heart-strings</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***схваченный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:схваченный.html>схва́ченный</a> (1074)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:схема.html>схе́ма</a> (3104)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:схема.html>схе́ма</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sxéma</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:схема.html>схе́мы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:схема.html>схе́мы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:схема.html>схе́м</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>scheme, layout, plan, outline</li>

<li>circuit</li>
<li>stereotyped pattern, pattern</li></ol>
